29.1(1): sku sangs rgyas thob/ thugs nyid zhi ba'i ngang tshul las/ thugs rjes nga rgyal 'khros 
29.2(1): tshul 'byin/ yang byed g.yo ba'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs/ gar gsas rol pa khro bo'i sku/
29.3(1): kun skyong sgrol ma yum dang sbyor/ nga rgyal 'khor ba dbyings su sgrol/ mnyam nyid ye 
29.4(1): shes bcud la rol/ sbyor sgrol rol pa'i 'du 'phro yis/ 'du byed phung po ngo bo grub/
29.5(1): lha ni gar gsas btsan po'i lha/ rigs ni byang phyogs las kyi rigs/ stobs ni zhi 
29.6(1): ba chen po'i stobs/ phrin las nga rgyal dregs pa 'joms/ spyan ni rnam dag chen 
29.7(1): po'i spyan/ gzigs ni sprul pa'i klong du gzigs/ lha sku rigs stobs ye shes kyis/
29.8(1): longs spyod rdzogs sku sangs rgyas thob/ thugs nyid so so'i ngang tshul las/ thugs 
29.9(1): rjes chags pa'i 'khros tshul 'byin/ gsal byed 'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs/
29.10(1): gnam gsas rol pa khro bo'i sku/ kun gsal smin ma yum dang sbyor/ 'dod chags 
29.11(1): 'khor ba dbyings su sgrol/ sor rtogs ye shes bcud la rol/ sbyor sgrol rol pa'i 
29.12(1): 'du 'phro yis/ tshor ba'i phung po sprul sku grub/ lha ni gnam gsas dbyings rum lha/
29.13(1): rigs ni nub phyogs pad+ma rigs/ stobs ni sbyin pa chen po'i stobs/ ye shes sor 
29.14(1): rtogs 'od po che/ phrin las 'dod chags rgya mtsho skems/ spyan ni shes rab chen 
29.15(1): po'i spyan/ gzigs ni snang srid 'khor 'das gzigs/ lha sku rigs stobs ye shes 
29.16(1): kyis/ longs spyod rdzogs sku'i sangs rgyas thob/ thugs nyid yangs pa'i ngang tshul 
29.17(1): las/ thugs rjes phrag dog 'khros tshul 'byin/ kun gso brlan byed dkyil 'khor 
29.18(1): rdzogs/ rgod gsas rol pa'i khro bo'i sku/ kun bsdud dbang mo yum dang sbyor/ phrag 
29.19(1): dog 'khor ba dbyings su sgrol/ bya nan ye shes bcud la rol/ sbyor sgrol rol ba'i 
29.20(1): 'du 'phro yis/ 'du shes phung po mngon byang grub/ lha ni rgod gsas khams pa'i lha/
29.21(1): rigs ni lho phyogs rin chen rigs/ stobs ni yangs pa chen po'i stobs/ ye shes 
30.1(1): bya nan 'od po che/ phrin las phrag dog brtson ra bshigs/ spyan ni thugs rje chen 
30.2(1): po'i spyan/ gzigs ni 'gro ba'i don la gzigs/ lha sku rigs stobs ye shes kyis/

30.4(1): ba sngags kyi don ldan nas/ sngags kyi 'bras bu thob par 'gyur/ bsdus pa'i rim 
30.5(1): pa ci ltar na/ thugs rje 'khros pa'i bzhin tshul rnams/ thugs nyid zhi ba'i klong du 
30.6(1): bsdus/ zhe sdang byams pa'i klong du bsdu/ gti mug ye shes klong du bsdu/ nga rgyal zhi 
30.7(1): ba'i dbyings su bsdu/ 'dod chags sbyin pa'i klong du bsdu/ phrag dog yangs nga

30.9(1): yon ro gcig klong du mnyam/ gnyis su med par gnyis med ston/ rtag chad 
30.10(1): mtshan mar gnyis mtha' bral/ yangs dog mtha' la rnam par gnas/ khro rgyal 
30.11(1): dbyings kyi lta ba yin/ 'chi med gtsug phud sprul pa'i gshen/ bsdus pa'i rim pa 
30.12(1): de ltar ro/ /khro bo'i rgyal po srid gsum rje/ gsang mchog rgyal po mthar thug bon/
30.13(1): bsnyen sgrub las gsum sngags kyi rgyud/ las skal ldan pa khyod la gtad/ khyed kyi 
30.14(1): go rim ma nor ba/ mi 'chor yid la dam du zungs/ ma brjed thugs kyi dkyil du

30.17(1): 'dus te/ mi snang bar gyur nas/ mdun gyi bar snang la/ gzhal yas khang 'od kyi 
30.18(1): gur khang du/ pad+ma'i gdan la/ thugs nyid zhi ba'i ngang tshul du bzhugs so/ /pha rgyud 
30.19(1): rig pa khu byug gsang mchog mthar thug rgyal po/ rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ dbal chen po 
30.20(1): 'phros pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su spros bsdus mdzad pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// //
30.21(1): 7 de nas yang de yi tshe/ gshen 'chi med gtsug phud kyis/ dngos 'byor gyi

48.2(1): pa yi/ rgyal ba dkyil 'khor lha tshogs la/ sgrub gshen mched dang lcam dral gyis/
48.3(1): lus ngag yid gsum gus phyag 'tshal/ lus ni gus pa lnga ldan te/ ngag ni spro ba'i
